posted:Posted March 30, 2024
msg:Ok I got a lot to say about the Mandarin Oriental Shenzhen - a hotel with luxurious amenities but lacking basic breakfast provisions‚Ä¶

Dyson hair drier, toto washlet, glass bottled water are all under expected. MO shenzhen used very highend sanitary fitting brands, reliable and taken very good care of. I am very picky on sanitary fittings and cleanliness and I have not noticed any issues. Kudos to the housekeeping team.

One must understand what sets MO apart from other hotels is the impeccable attention to details. Its interior design is far superior to other Shenzhen hotels. If you are architecture fan and are tired of the substandard detailing in other Shenzhen hotels please do try MO shenzhen.

Now‚Ä¶ the problem for me was with the breakfast. It occurred to me that MO focused way too much on cantonese food and was probably swayed by foreigner‚Äôs perception of what ‚Äúoriental culture‚Äù consists of. Granted that the food was of high quality - good sauce good ingredients. But it is rly rly rly basic to provide rice. In every top hotels I visited around Asia, I never had to miss fried rice. It was very dissimilar experience in MO compared to Ritz carlton I stayed few weeks before - who probably had 3 times more variety of offerings. I wouldnt hesitate to pay extra if there was a better breakfast offering - as many would understand that this is just attitude issue.

The greatest hotel service in Asia. MO group is known for this and I cannot agree more. I knew of this ever since many years ago when I was in Guangzhou MO next to Taikoo.

Overall, as said earlier, MO shenzhen gave me mixed feelings. I am astounded by the cleanliness, detailing but I cannot hop on the MO Fan boat yet because of the breakfast. Aiya!

name:S‚Äçu‚Äçn‚Äçn‚Äçy‚ÄçH‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äç0‚Äç0‚Äç7

posted:Posted September 23, 2022
msg:Dear friends of Mandarin Oriental, Shenzhen, here comes the comment Mr. Xu owes you for a long time!
First of all, thank you very much for your caring care over the past few months!
Next is the comment section!

Overall: Mandarin Oriental is located in the business district of Shum Yip Upper City. To be honest, this location is a bit desolate, and it is like a lonely king standing here. Fortunately, there is still a business district downstairs, and you can still eat, drink and play. In addition, because it is opened in 2022, it is really new!

Transportation: The transportation is generally convenient, you have to take a taxi or drive by yourself. Affected by the deep design problem, and the hotel is relatively new, I did encounter many small problems when taking a taxi. For example, the master does not know the road, or the positioning of the online car-hailing is wrong. So here are some tips for you.
If you are going to Wenhua, remember to tell the master to go up to the back of the second floor, many masters will go up, but generally you will think that you are going to Wuyin, and then let the master keep driving forward to become Wenhua.
If you start from Wenhua, you can often encounter taxis on the side of the road. Or take a few more steps and go down from the mall to the first floor, and there are many taxis lining up waiting for customers. If it is an online car-hailing, the special car usually knows Wenhua, and will drive up to the entrance of the lobby on the second floor by itself. But if it is an express train, I often encounter the master parked downstairs, and I have encountered it a few times. Therefore, if it is a big express car, it will be more convenient to locate it in the Porsche 4s store.
If you drive by yourself, you have to go to the entrance in front of the Wenhua entrance on the second floor and go to the parking lot. The hotel provides free parking. When you want to drive out, report the license plate number at the front desk. However, it is actually quite troublesome to have to complain about driving, because it is a little long to go down from the other side, but this is also a design problem and there is no way.

Check-in: The lobby of Wenhua is on the 78th floor. The lobby area is not large, but it is very comfortable inside. There are three counters on the left and right, and there should be no problem during peak hours. There is a restaurant on the same floor, and there is a small bar in the lounge? forgotten. After check-in, unlike many other high-rise hotels, Shenzhen Wenhua's rooms are to go down, not up, which is very interesting.

Room: I have been booking a deluxe king bed on Ctrip and then upgraded to a room type with a premium king bed for free, and I have also been upgraded to an executive suite. Therefore, the deluxe double room type cannot be evaluated. The area of reward and administrative facilities is similar. The only difference is the orientation. The executive can see the sea. It is also equipped with a telescope. Look at the safety of the opposite side, and during the day you can watch the helicopter land on the Greater China (I am really bored). Other room types will have the opportunity to experience and write for your reference in the future.

Facilities: The facilities outside the room are basically complete. The spa, swimming pool and gym are on the 68th floor. I have never experienced the spa. Steam, jacuzzi, both, not bad. The gym has not been used but visited, as training for daily travel is sufficient. In addition, Mobar is on the 79th floor, you can experience it, the scenery is good, and the wine is also good, but the epidemic may not be open now, and the above should not be open.
In the room, the Dyson hair dryer is not a novelty, nor is the Nespresso coffee machine. The bath set is from Tiptik. It smells like no fragrant fruit, but I always feel like it smells like coconut, but it's more comfortable with Guangzhou Mandarin's Oulong citrus. The most worthy of praise is the toothpaste. In the early days, I used terra toothpaste, which is actually very easy to use, but it is very easy to dry after opening. Later, it was replaced by Marvis, which was much better.

Service: There is nothing to say about service. If Wenhua is the second in the industry, it is estimated that whoever wants to be the first will have to weigh carefully. From the lobby on the second floor to the lobby of 78, the staff I encountered were very enthusiastic. The point is here. First of all, I praised Rachael at the front desk. She cared about me very much when she was still in office. I met her at check-in many times. Although she has left her job now, she is still very helpful when you have any questions. Next up is Shawn and Neil, old pals, and they've been together a lot. The other is the Guest Experience Center. This time, I celebrated my girlfriend's birthday this time. The communication in the early stage was very smooth. I especially praised Aggie and Even. I spent a lot of effort in setting up the celebration.

Service: Mandarin Oriental's personalized service is not fixed, it is really in place, as long as the demand is not excessive, it can basically satisfy you. There is also a night service, which will prepare slippers and adjust the lights in advance and wait for you to go back. The other is the locker, which is very user-friendly, there are many inconvenient situations, you can let the room service put it in the locker, and then go to get it.

Overall: Mandarin Oriental is my yyds, there are not many pictures, because it is too new, so just refer to the official pictures.

posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:During the May Day holiday, I booked a two-night stay at the Mandarin Oriental Shenzhen through Ctrip Live. The package clearly included two adult breakfasts and a customized dinner. After confirming these details with Ctrip customer service, I completed the reservation.

However, when I arrived at the hotel and checked in, the front desk informed me that the package did not include dinner, only breakfast. This discrepancy disappointed me. Nevertheless, in order not to let this matter affect our vacation, we decided not to dwell on it. However, on the second night of dining at the hotel, we ran into Mr. Liang in the hotel lobby. Mr. Liang took the initiative to upgrade our room to a higher floor and a larger room type. Although we were going to check out the next day, he generously delayed our check-out time, accommodated our travel plans, provided a welcome fruit plate, personally helped us move to the new room, and assisted us with our luggage.

It is worth mentioning that the Dongwan Restaurant on the first floor of the hotel. This was our second visit to the restaurant in two days. The dishes recommended by Manager Wang were very much to our taste, especially the two desserts that were "bottom of the box" in their restaurant, which were not only visually eye-catching, but also a wonderful challenge for the taste buds. The delicious enjoyment and experience made us decide that we would definitely come back for the third time.

Finally, Ctrip also responded and we were satisfied. Although this experience had its ups and downs, it was a satisfying accommodation experience overall. üëçüèª
